    SELECT b.id, b.booking_type, b.cancelled_at, b.confirmed_at, b.created_at, b.created_by_user_id, b.deleted_at, b.deleted_by_user_id, b.end_date, b.guests_count, b.is_deleted, b.notes, b.quantity, b.reference_id, b.start_date, b.status, b.total_price, b.updated_at, b.updated_by_user_id, b.user_id
    FROM bookings AS b
    WHERE NOT (b.is_deleted) AND b.user_id = @__userId_Value_0
    ORDER BY b.created_at DESC
    LIMIT @__p_2 OFFSET @__p_1
) AS b0
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT u.id, u.created_at, u.created_by_user_id, u.deleted_at, u.deleted_by_user_id, u.email, u.email_confirmed, u.full_name, u.is_active, u.is_deleted, u.last_login_at, u.password_hash, u.phone_number, u.role, u.updated_at, u.updated_by_user_id
    FROM users AS u
    WHERE NOT (u.is_deleted)
) AS u0 ON b0.user_id = u0.id
ORDER BY b0.created_at DESC
